template <typename T>






172



constexpr inline T sin_using_table_256(size_t k);






173









174



template <>






175



constexpr inline f32 sin_using_table_256<f32>(size_t k)






176



{






177



    return (k == 0 || k == 128) ? 0.f






178



                                : (k == 64) ? 1.f








loop-vectorize

                                     
 loop not vectorized: loop control flow is not understood by vectorizer 		
float kfr::sin_using_table_256(unsigned long)







loop-vectorize

                                     
 loop not vectorized 		
float kfr::sin_using_table_256(unsigned long)





179



                                            : (k > 128) ? -sin_using_table_256<f32>(k - 128)

                                                        : (k > 64) ? sin_using_table_256<f32>(128 - k)

                                                                   : data::c_sin_table_f32[k];






182



}

template <typename T>






194



constexpr inline T sin_using_table(size_t size, size_t k)






195



{






196



    return sin_using_table_256<T>((k * 256 / size) % 256);








inline
